# ---- start of include part ----
NUM_SLOTS = 1
SLOT_TYPE_1 = cpus=$(GLIDEIN_CPUS)
NUM_SLOTS_TYPE_1 = 1
SLOT_TYPE_1_PARTITIONABLE = True
STARTD_SLOT_ATTRS = State, Activity, EnteredCurrentActivity, TotalTimeUnclaimedIdle, TotalTimeClaimedBusy

DS1_TO_DIE = ((GLIDEIN_ToDie =!= UNDEFINED) && (CurrentTime > GLIDEIN_ToDie))

# The condition pre 8.2 is valid only for not partitionable slots
# Since the idle timer doesn't reset/stop when resources are reclaimed, 
# partitionable slots will get reaped sooner than non-partitionable.
DS1_NOT_PARTITIONABLE = ((PartitionableSlot =!= True) || (TotalSlots =?=1))
# The daemon shutdown expression for idle startds(glideins) depends on some conditions:
# If some jobs were sheduled on the startd (TAIL) or none at all (NOJOB)
# If using condor 8.2 or later (NEW) or previous versions (PRE82). JobStarts defined
# is used to discriminate
DS1_IS_HTCONDOR_NEW = (Slot1_JobStarts =!= UNDEFINED)
# No jobs started (using GLIDEIN_Max_Idle) 
DS1_IDLE_NOJOB_NEW = ((Slot1_JobStarts =!= UNDEFINED) && (Slot1_SelfMonitorAge =!= UNDEFINED) && (GLIDEIN_Max_Idle =!= UNDEFINED) && \
                  (Slot1_JobStarts == 0) && \
                  (Slot1_SelfMonitorAge > GLIDEIN_Max_Idle))
DS1_IDLE_NOJOB_PRE82 = ((Slot1_TotalTimeUnclaimedIdle =!= UNDEFINED) && (GLIDEIN_Max_Idle =!= UNDEFINED) && \
        $(DS1_NOT_PARTITIONABLE) && \
        (Slot1_TotalTimeUnclaimedIdle > GLIDEIN_Max_Idle))
DS1_IDLE_NOJOB = ((GLIDEIN_Max_Idle =!= UNDEFINED) && \
        ifThenElse($(DS1_IS_HTCONDOR_NEW), $(DS1_IDLE_NOJOB_NEW), $(DS1_IDLE_NOJOB_PRE82))) 
# Some jobs started (using GLIDEIN_Max_Tail)
DS1_IDLE_TAIL_NEW = ((Slot1_JobStarts =!= UNDEFINED) && (Slot1_ExpectedMachineGracefulDrainingCompletion =!= UNDEFINED) && (GLIDEIN_Max_Tail =!= UNDEFINED) && \
        (Slot1_JobStarts > 0) && \
        ((CurrentTime - Slot1_ExpectedMachineGracefulDrainingCompletion) > GLIDEIN_Max_Tail) )
DS1_IDLE_TAIL_PRE82 = ((Slot1_TotalTimeUnclaimedIdle =!= UNDEFINED) && (GLIDEIN_Max_Tail =!= UNDEFINED) && \
        (Slot1_TotalTimeClaimedBusy =!= UNDEFINED) && \
        $(DS1_NOT_PARTITIONABLE) && \
        (Slot1_TotalTimeUnclaimedIdle > GLIDEIN_Max_Tail))
DS1_IDLE_TAIL = ((GLIDEIN_Max_Tail =!= UNDEFINED) && \
        ifThenElse($(DS1_IS_HTCONDOR_NEW), $(DS1_IDLE_TAIL_NEW), $(DS1_IDLE_TAIL_PRE82)))
DS1_IDLE_RETIRE = ($(DS1_NOT_PARTITIONABLE) && (GLIDEIN_ToRetire =!= UNDEFINED) && \
       (CurrentTime > GLIDEIN_ToRetire ))
DS1_IDLE = ( (Slot1_Activity == "Idle") && \
        ($(DS1_IDLE_NOJOB) || $(DS1_IDLE_TAIL) || $(DS1_IDLE_RETIRE)) )

DS1 = ($(DS1_TO_DIE) || \
          $(DS1_IDLE))

# But don't enforce shutdowns for dynamic slots (aka "subslots")
DS1 = (DynamicSlot =!= True) && ($(DS1))

STARTD.DAEMON_SHUTDOWN =  $(DS1)
######################################################################
##
##  condor_config.dedicated_starter.include
##
##  Condor include file for main starter 
##
######################################################################

WORK_DIR=$(LOCAL_DIR)

# No need to be nice... I got the slot
JOB_RENICE_INCREMENT = 0

HAS_MONITOR_VM=True
IS_MONITOR_VM = False
USES_MONITOR_STARTD = True

STARTD_ATTRS = $(STARTD_ATTRS), IS_MONITOR_VM, HAS_MONITOR_VM, USES_MONITOR_STARTD, Monitoring_Name

GLIDEIN_REQUIREMENTS = ((GLIDEIN_ToRetire =?= UNDEFINED) || (CurrentTime < GLIDEIN_ToRetire))

START = ($(GLIDEIN_START_CONDITION)) && ($(GLIDEIN_REQUIREMENTS))
WANT_HOLD = ($(GLIDEIN_HOLD_CONDITION))
PREEMPT = (($(GLIDEIN_HOLD_CONDITION)) || ($(GLIDEIN_PREEMPT_CONDITION)))

IsOwner = False

# Max time a job is guaranteed to run in the glidein
# set it to several months... i.e. infinity
# (unless we are vacating a held job then should be zero)
MaxJobRetirementTime=ifthenelse(($(WANT_HOLD))=!=True,$(PREEMPT_GRACE_TIME),$(HOLD_GRACE_TIME))

# How long does the job have after the startd enters retiring state
SHUTDOWN_GRACEFUL_TIMEOUT=$(GLIDEIN_Graceful_Shutdown)

# How long will it wait in an unclaimed state before exiting
STARTD_NOCLAIM_SHUTDOWN = $(GLIDEIN_Max_Idle)

# Shutdown the master if the startd exits.  Note that if
# STARTD_StartTime is zero, that the startd is not currently running.
#
MASTER.DAEMON_SHUTDOWN = (STARTD_StartTime =?= 0)

# Make sure subslots get renegotiated
CLAIM_WORKLIFE = ifThenElse(DynamicSlot =?= True, $(GLIDEIN_CLAIM_WORKLIFE_DYNAMIC), $(GLIDEIN_CLAIM_WORKLIFE))
